Any endpoint\n   *                              that does not appear in this map will be started once all\n   *                              authorizerFutures are complete.\n   *\n   * @return                      A future which is completed when all of the acceptor threads have\n   *                              successfully started. non-blocking multi-connection network I/O. It works with NetworkSend and NetworkReceive to transmit size-delimited network requests and responses.\\n\\n2. **Byte Buffer Management** (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/network/):\\n   - NetworkReceive.java: Implements the Receive interface for managing incoming byte buffers\\n   - NetworkSend.java: Implements the Send interface for managing outgoing byte buffers\\n   - ByteBufferSend.java: A concrete Send implementation for ByteBuffer-based message transmission\\n\\n3. **KafkaChannel** (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/network/KafkaChannel.java): Encapsulates communication with a single remote node, wrapping the low-level SocketChannel and coordinating with the Selector.\\n\\n4. **Server-side Architecture** (core/src/main/scala/kafka/network/):\\n   - SocketServer.scala: The main server socket handler that manages the complete request/response flow:\\n     - SocketServer class: Orchestrates the entire network layer, manages multiple listeners (data-plane, control-plane), and coordinates acceptors and processors\\n     - DataPlaneAcceptor class: Handles incoming connections for data-plane listeners\\n     - Acceptor abstract class: Base abstraction for accepting new socket connections and handing them off to Processor threads\\n     - Processor class: Runs in dedicated threads, handles reads from sockets using the Selector and writes responses back\\n   \\n   - RequestChannel.scala: The handoff mechanism between Processor threads and request handler threads:\\n     - RequestChannel class: Provides thread-safe queues for passing requests from Processors to handlers and responses back\\n     - Request class: Encapsulates a network request with metadata and buffer management\\n\\n5. **Supporting Components**:\\n   - Selectable.java: Interface defining the contract for socket-aware selectable objects\\n   - Receive.java: Interface for receiving network data\\n   - Send.java: Interface for sending network data\\n   - TransportLayer.java: Abstraction for transport-level I/O operations\\n   - ChannelBuilder.java: Factory interface for creating configured channels\\n   - RequestChannelMetrics.java: Metrics collection for the RequestChannel\\n\\nThe flow proceeds as: Client connections → Acceptor threads (per listener) → Processor threads (with Selector) → RequestChannel → Handler threads → Response back through Processor threads → Selector → NetworkSend → Socket.\\n\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[{"oldStart":67,"oldLines":6,"newStart":67,"newLines":18,"lines":["     {","       \"repo\": \"apache/kafka\",","       \"path\": \"clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/network/SslChannelBuilder.java\"","+    },","+    {","+      \"repo\": \"apache/kafka\",","+      \"path\": \"server/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/network/RequestConvertToJson.java\"","+    },","+    {","+      \"repo\": \"apache/kafka\",","+      \"path\": \"server/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/network/Session.java\"","+    },","+    {","+      \"repo\": \"apache/kafka\",","+      \"path\": \"server/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/network/SocketServerConfigs.java\"","     }","   ],","   \"symbols\": ["]}],"userModified":false,"replaceAll":false}}

interconnected components across the codebase:\\n\\n1. **NIO-based Selector** (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/network/Selector.java): The core NIO selector implementation that handles non-blocking multi-connection network I/O. It works with NetworkSend and NetworkReceive to transmit size-delimited network requests and responses.\\n\\n2. **Byte Buffer Management** (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/network/):\\n   - NetworkReceive.java: Implements the Receive interface for managing incoming byte buffers\\n   - NetworkSend.java: Implements the Send interface for managing outgoing byte buffers\\n   - ByteBufferSend.java: A concrete Send implementation for ByteBuffer-based message transmission\\n\\n3. **KafkaChannel** (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/network/KafkaChannel.java): Encapsulates communication with a single remote node, wrapping the low-level SocketChannel and coordinating with the Selector.\\n\\n4. **Server-side Architecture** (core/src/main/scala/kafka/network/):\\n   - SocketServer.scala: The main server socket handler that manages the complete request/response flow:\\n     - SocketServer class: Orchestrates the entire network layer, manages multiple listeners (data-plane, control-plane), and coordinates acceptors and processors\\n     - DataPlaneAcceptor class: Handles incoming connections for data-plane listeners\\n     - Acceptor abstract class: Base abstraction for accepting new socket connections and handing them off to Processor threads\\n     - Processor class: Runs in dedicated threads, handles reads from sockets using the Selector and writes responses back\\n   \\n   - RequestChannel.scala: The handoff mechanism between Processor threads and request handler threads:\\n     - NetworkReceive.java: Implements the Receive interface for managing incoming byte buffers\\n   - NetworkSend.java: Implements the Send interface for managing outgoing byte buffers\\n   - ByteBufferSend.java: A concrete Send implementation for ByteBuffer-based message transmission\\n\\n3. **KafkaChannel** (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/network/KafkaChannel.java): Encapsulates communication with a single remote node, wrapping the low-level SocketChannel and coordinating with the Selector.\\n\\n4. **Server-side Architecture** (core/src/main/scala/kafka/network/):\\n   - DataPlaneAcceptor class: Handles incoming connections for data-plane listeners\\n     - Acceptor abstract class: Base abstraction for accepting new socket connections and handing them off to Processor threads\\n     - interconnected components across the codebase:\\n\\n1. **NIO-based Selector** (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/network/Selector.java): The core NIO selector implementation that handles non-blocking multi-connection network I/O. It works with NetworkSend and NetworkReceive to transmit size-delimited network requests and responses.\\n\\n2. **Byte Buffer Management** (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/network/):\\n   - NetworkReceive.java: Implements the Receive interface for managing incoming byte buffers\\n   - NetworkSend.java: Implements the Send interface for managing outgoing byte buffers\\n   - ByteBufferSend.java: A concrete Send implementation for ByteBuffer-based message transmission\\n\\n3. **KafkaChannel** (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/network/KafkaChannel.java): Encapsulates communication with a single remote node, wrapping the low-level SocketChannel and coordinating with the Selector.\\n\\n4. **Server-side Architecture** (core/src/main/scala/kafka/network/):\\n   - SocketServer.scala: The main server socket handler that manages the complete request/response flow:\\n     - SocketServer class: Orchestrates the entire network layer, manages multiple listeners (data-plane, control-plane), and coordinates acceptors and processors\\n     - DataPlaneAcceptor class: Handles incoming connections for data-plane listeners\\n     - Acceptor abstract class: Base abstraction for accepting new socket connections and handing them off to Processor threads\\n     - Processor class: Runs in dedicated threads, handles reads from sockets using the Selector and writes responses back\\n   \\n   - RequestChannel.scala: The handoff mechanism between Processor threads and request handler threads:\\n     - RequestChannel class: Provides thread-safe queues for passing requests from Processors to handlers and responses back\\n     - Request class: Encapsulates a network request with metadata and buffer management\\n\\n5. **Supporting Components**:\\n   - Selectable.java: Interface defining the contract for socket-aware selectable objects\\n   - Receive.java: Interface for receiving network data\\n   - Send.java: Interface for sending network data\\n   - TransportLayer.java: Abstraction for transport-level I/O operations\\n   - ChannelBuilder.java: Factory interface for creating configured channels\\n   - RequestChannelMetrics.java: Metrics collection for the RequestChannel\\n\\nThe flow proceeds as: Client connections → Acceptor threads (per listener) → Processor threads (with Selector) → RequestChannel → Handler threads → Response back through Processor threads → Selector → NetworkSend → Socket.\\n\"\n}\n","numLines":224,"startLine":1,"totalLines":224}}}
